<script>
    var countdownEl = document.getElementById("countdown");
    var countdownBtn = document.getElementById("countdown-btn");
    var copyBtn = document.getElementById("copy-btn");
    var countdownFinished = false;

    countdownBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        var count = 82;
        countdownBtn.disabled = true;
        var countdown = setInterval(function () {
            countdownBtn.innerHTML = "Pass hiển thị sau: " + count;
            count--;
            if (count < 0) {
                clearInterval(countdown);
                countdownBtn.innerHTML = "modgame123";
                countdownEl.innerHTML = "modgame123";
                countdownFinished = true;
                showCopyBtn();
            }
        }, 1000);
    });

    function showCopyBtn() {
        if (countdownFinished) {
            copyBtn.style.display = "block";
        }
    }

    copyBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        var text = countdownEl.innerText;
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
        copyBtn.innerHTML = "Đã sao chép!";
    });

	function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
		var d = new Date();
		d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
		var expires = "expires="+ d.toUTCString();
